1a:T898,<p><b>Dragon Ball Z </b>Statue of <b>Bojack </b>in <b>Movies Collection,</b> 1/4 scale size approx.63cm. <strong>Official product</strong> in <strong>limited edition of 700 pieces</strong> by <strong>Tsume Art</strong>.</p>
<p>The Dragon Ball Z Movies Collection continues with a new release: Bojack Unbound, featuring an imposing Bojack DBZ statue dedicated to the iconic antagonist from the movie. This statue Dragon Ball Z captures the sheer power and intimidating presence of the galactic pirate, making it an essential piece for any fan.</p>
<p>This piece from the Dragon Ball Z statue collection brings Bojack to life with incredible detail. His imposing posture and precisely sculpted face reflect his charisma and menacing demeanor. Every element contributes to recreating the tension of one of the most intense battles in the DBZ saga.</p>
<p>Why is this piece a must-have?</p>
<ul>
<li>A perfectly sculpted face: Bojack is depicted in all his glory, with detailed features, a chilling expression, and piercing eyes that capture his menacing aura.</li>
<li>A massive statue: Standing at 63 cm tall, this statue commands an impressive presence, paying homage to one of DBZ's greatest threats.</li>
<li>Breathtaking details: From his clothing to his accessories and finely textured jewelry, every aspect of this statue has been crafted to deliver a spectacular result.</li>
</ul>
<p>The Movies Collection continues…</p>
<p>Bojack marks the second statue in the Dragon Ball Z Movies Collection, and many more iconic characters are coming to complete this series. Stay tuned to find out who will be next to join this incredible collection!</p>
<p><span style="text-decoration:underline;"><strong>Movies Collection:</strong></span></p>
<p>Tsume's Movies Collection is an invitation to rediscover the world of Dragon Ball in a whole new light. Featuring highlights from the films, this collection allows fans to relive the epic battles and memorable scenes that have shaped the Dragon Ball legend. With 15 years' experience and an unwavering commitment to quality, Tsume continues to push back the boundaries of creation to offer enthusiasts unique and exceptional collector's items.</p>1b:T5d6,<p><b>Dragon Ball Z </b>Statue of <b>Super Saiyan 3 Gotenks </b>in <b>HQS Dioramax,</b> 1/6 scale size approx.48cm. <strong>Official product</strong> in <strong>limited edition of 800 pieces</strong> by <strong>Tsume Art</strong>.</p>
<p>This new HQS Dioramax from Tsume in the Dragon Ball Z license captures all the power and exuberance of Gotenks in his Super Saiyan 3 form, during his Kamikaze Ghost attack. This dynamic scene showcases the hero as he summons his famous Kamikaze Ghosts. Every detail of the scene is designed to recreate the intensity of the moment, with Gotenks charging towards the enemy accompanied by his ghosts!</p>

<p>The scenery is rich in detail, immersing the scene in an epic atmosphere. Each element is finely sculpted, bringing depth and realism to the whole.</p>

Times-three Kaio-ken KAMEHAME-HA !!!!"-<strong> Son Goku</strong><br /><br />Relive the first encounter and first clash on Earth between Son Goku, the hero of Dragon Ball Z and Vegeta, the Prince of Saiyans, through the realization of an explosive 1/6 HQS statue!<br /><br />Although these two protagonists share the same origins, they do not share the same purpose, since everything opposes them, especially their convictions! The ruthless anti-hero wants to prove his incontestable superiority at all costs by destroying the planet, its inhabitants and adversary, while the Earths great defender intends to use all his strength to prevent it, fed by a destructive desire for revenge. There is only one solution: to engage in a merciless fight May the strongest win!<br /><br />Determined to protect his family and avenge his friends, Son Goku is determined to let his rage out! In reality, he has no choice, he cannot fail: on his victory depends the survival of humanity. We see him here deploying all his strength and energy to fight and try to defeat the space warrior and Saiyans prince, preparing a fearsome attack taught by his master Kaiō-sama: the Kaio-ken x3! An overpowering and destructive attack that forces him to push his limits, thereby putting his own life in danger!<br /><br />We recognize the place of the clash thanks to the terracotta desert ground painted in a gradation of brown, orange and reddish shades, while we notice that the rocks rise in the air due to the immeasurable energy exerted by Son Goku. He will do everything in his power to save his loved ones this time around: the titanic effort he generates is transcribed through the fierce expression of his grimacing face as well as the muscles of his overdeveloped chest ready to tear themselves apart. The Saiyans super massive and protruding musculature is underlined by the light and shadow effects performed by our painters, while the reddish aura enveloping his entire figure manifests his transformation.<br /><br />The warrior wears his usual orange trousers tightened at the waist by his blue belt floating in the air under the effect of the attack, like his dark hair. His orange and navy blue shoes sink into the ground to stabilize themselves by accumulating as much energy as possible. Cracking the ground under the effect of the energy deployed, legs spread, arms outstretched, he is about to unleash all his power to remind his assailant of the reason why he should never have set foot on this planet. We then see him forming with his hands a sphere of energy in translucent resin in shades of blue, while the immense aura of energy in translucent red resin behind him and the dust suddenly rising from the ground testify to the strength of the shock caused by the attack intended to wipe his opponent from the face of the earth!<br /><br />The blue sphere of energy can be placed or not in the palm of Son Goku's hands thanks to its interchangeable arms, thus showing the Saiyan preparing his attack or even attacking, especially if he is placed in front of the Vegeta HQS statue associated, in order to bring the combat between the two super warriors to life.
